019909,003490:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019910,003491: 
019911,003492:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019912,003493:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019913,003494:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019914,003495:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019915,003496: 
019916,003497:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019917,003498:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019918,003499:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019919,003500:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019920,003501:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019921,003502:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019922,003503:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019923,003504: 
019924,003505:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019925,003506:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019926,003507:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019927,003508:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019928,003509:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019929,003510: 
019930,003511:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019931,003512:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019932,003513:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019933,003514:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019934,003515:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019935,003516: 
019936,003517:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019937,003518:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019938,003519:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019939,003520: 
019940,003521: 
019941,003522:                                                                                                  #  .
019942,003523: 
019943,003524:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019944,003525:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019945,003526:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019946,003527:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019947,003528: 
019948,003529:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019949,003530:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019950,003531:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019951,003532:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019952,003533:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019953,003534:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 464 

019955,003536:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019956,003537: 
019957,003538:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019958,003539:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019959,003540:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019960,003541:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019961,003542:    4443           10647                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019962,003543:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019963,003544: 
019964,003545:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019965,003546:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019966,003547: 
019967,003548: 04,2647                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019968,003549: 04,2647                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019969,003550: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019970,003551: 04,2650           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019971,003552: 04,2651           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019972,003553: 04,2652           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019973,003554: 04,2653           30001                           CA       L                                     
019974,003555: 04,2654           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019975,003556: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019976,003557: 
019977,003558:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019978,003559:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019979,003560:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019980,003561:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019981,003562:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019982,003563: 
019983,003564:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019984,003565:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019985,003566:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019986,003567:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019987,003568:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019988,003569:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019989,003570:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019990,003571:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019991,003572:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019992,003573:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019993,003574:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019994,003575:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019995,003576:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019996,003577: 
019997,003578:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019998,003579:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019999,003580:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
020000,003581: 
020001,003582:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
020002,003583:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
020003,003584:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

Page 465 

020005,003586:    4462           00004                           INHINT                                         
020006,003587:    4463           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
020007,003588:    4464           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
020008,003589:    4465           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
020009,003590:    4466           04470                           TC       +2                                    
020010,003591:    4467           04473                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
020011,003592:    4470           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  
020012,003593:    4471           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
020013,003594:    4472           05137                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
020014,003595:    4473           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
020015,003596:    4474           44747                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
020016,003597:    4475           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)

020145,003726:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF:
020146,003727:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020147,003728:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020148,003729:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020149,003730:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020150,003731:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020151,003732:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
